    ("Instance.rawpsubst_compose_freshVar2_aux",
     "[| ?\<phi> : UNIV; set ?ts <= UNIV; set ?xs <= UNIV; distinct ?xs;
         set ?us <= UNIV; distinct ?us; set ?us Int Fvars ?\<phi> = {};
         set ?us Int \<Union> (Fvars ` set ?ts) = {};
         set ?us Int set ?xs = {}; set ?vs <= UNIV; distinct ?vs;
         set ?vs Int Fvars ?\<phi> = {};
         set ?vs Int \<Union> (Fvars ` set ?ts) = {};

         length ?vs = length ?xs; length ?ts = length ?xs;
